	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Help:Multilingual support</h1>
	
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"><div class="mw-revision warningbox"><div id="mw-revision-info-current"><p><b>This is the <a href="/wiki/Help:Page_history" title="Help:Page history">current revision</a> of this page, as edited by <span id="mw-revision-name"><a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Rossen2&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new mw-userlink" title="User:Rossen2 (page does not exist)"><bdi>Rossen2</bdi></a> <span class="mw-usertoollinks">(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Rossen2" class="mw-usertoollinks-talk" title="User talk:Rossen2">talk</a> | <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Rossen2" class="mw-usertoollinks-contribs" title="Special:Contributions/Rossen2">contribs</a>)</span></span> at <span id="mw-revision-date">05:38, 6 February 2020</span><span id="mw-revision-summary"> <span class="comment">(<span dir="auto"><span class="autocomment"><a href="#Sharada">→‎Sharada</a></span></span>)</span></span>. 		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">For help for visitors to the English-language Wikipedia, see <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Local_embassy" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:Local embassy">Wikipedia:Local embassy</a>.</div> 
<table class="plainlinks ombox ombox-notice" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><a href="/wiki/File:Twemoji_1f527.svg" class="image"><img alt="Twemoji 1f527.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Twemoji_1f527.svg/30px-Twemoji_1f527.svg.png" decoding="async" width="30" height="30" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Twemoji_1f527.svg/45px-Twemoji_1f527.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Twemoji_1f527.svg/60px-Twemoji_1f527.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="512" /></a></td><td class="mbox-text"><div style="padding-top: 6px; padding-bottom: 5px;"><b>This help page is a <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Project_namespace#Wikipedia_how-to_and_information_pages" title="Wikipedia:Project namespace">how-to guide</a>.</b><br /><div style="font-size: 90%;">It details processes or procedures of some aspect(s) of Wikipedia's norms and practices. It is not one of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Policies_and_guidelines" title="Wikipedia:Policies and guidelines">Wikipedia's policies or guidelines</a>, as it has not been <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Consensus#Levels_of_consensus" title="Wikipedia:Consensus">thoroughly vetted by the community</a>.</div></div></td><td class="mbox-imageright"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r911143475">.mw-parser-output .module-shortcutboxplain{float:right;border:1px solid #aaa;background:#fff;margin:0 0 0 1em;padding:0.3em 0.6em 0.2em 0.6em;text-align:center;font-size:85%;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .module-shortcutlist{display:inline-block;border-bottom:1px solid #aaa;margin-bottom:0.2em;font-weight:normal}.mw-parser-output .module-shortcutanchordiv{position:relative;top:-3em}.mw-parser-output li .module-shortcutanchordiv{float:right}</style><div class="module-shortcutanchordiv"><span id="H:MS"></span></div><div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note"><div class="module-shortcutlist"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcut</a></div><ul><li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=H:MS&amp;redirect=no">H:MS</a></span></li></ul></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Articles on the English Wikipedia may contain words or texts written in different languages and scripts. To be able to correctly view and edit these articles requires that you have the appropriate <a href="/wiki/Font" title="Font">fonts</a> installed and to have correctly configured your <a href="/wiki/Operating_system" title="Operating system">operating system</a> and <a href="/wiki/Web_browser" title="Web browser">browser</a>. This guide will help you to do so.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Overview">Overview</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Overview">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Unicode">Unicode</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Unicode">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r911143475"/><div class="module-shortcutanchordiv"><span id="WP:UNICODE"></span></div><div class="module-shortcutboxplain plainlist noprint" role="note"><div class="module-shortcutlist"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Shortcut" title="Wikipedia:Shortcut">Shortcut</a></div><ul><li><span class="plainlinks"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Wikipedia:UNICODE&amp;redirect=no">WP:UNICODE</a></span></li></ul></div>
<p>Articles on Wikipedia are encoded using <a href="/wiki/Unicode" title="Unicode">Unicode</a> (specifically <a href="/wiki/UTF-8" title="UTF-8">UTF-8</a>)<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;a&#93;</a></sup>, an <a href="/wiki/Technical_standard" title="Technical standard">industry standard</a> designed to allow <a href="/wiki/Writing" title="Writing">text</a> and symbols from all of the <a href="/wiki/Writing_systems" class="mw-redirect" title="Writing systems">writing systems</a> of the world to be consistently represented and manipulated by <a href="/wiki/Computer" title="Computer">computers</a>. Because UTF-8 is <a href="/wiki/Backward_compatible" class="mw-redirect" title="Backward compatible">backward compatible</a> with <a href="/wiki/ASCII" title="ASCII">ASCII</a>, and most modern browsers have at least basic Unicode support, most users will experience little difficulty reading and editing most of Wikipedia.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Font">Font</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Font">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Unicode_font" title="Unicode font">Unicode font</a></div>
<p>Most computers with <a href="/wiki/Microsoft_Windows" title="Microsoft Windows">Microsoft Windows</a>, Apple's <a href="/wiki/MacOS" title="MacOS">macOS</a> and many <a href="/wiki/Linux" title="Linux">Linux</a> variants will already have fonts with support for Latin, Greek, Cyrillic, Hebrew, Arabic, Chinese, Japanese, Korean and the <a href="/wiki/International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="International Phonetic Alphabet">International Phonetic Alphabet</a> installed. Many mobile devices, such as the iPhone and iPad also include such fonts. Several historic and accented characters (used in the transliteration of foreign scripts) may be missing, though. 
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Microsoft_fonts">Microsoft fonts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Microsoft fonts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Browsers">Browsers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Browsers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dt>Internet Explorer</dt>
<dd>supports Latin (however not all extended sets), Greek, Cyrillic, Arabic and Hebrew. Support for East Asian and some Indic scripts is available if support for this has been installed for Windows. As Internet Explorer will only use the default font for other scripts, those are usually not supported (unless the default font does).</dd>
<dt>Firefox</dt>
<dd>tries to render any character using all the fonts available on the system so multilingual support is generally good. The default rendering engine can support complex script rendering. Some Linux distributions ship with a <a href="/wiki/Pango" title="Pango">Pango</a>-based rendering engine which also does, although this may currently cause some display glitches with justified text.</dd>
<dt>Opera</dt>
<dd>tries to render any character using all the fonts available on the system so multilingual support is also good.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> Opera uses the operating system to perform contextual glyph selection, ligature forming, character stacking, combining character support and other character shaping tasks.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup></dd>
<dt>Chrome</dt>
<dd>Does not directly support several languages of South and Southeast Asian countries, but otherwise renders some <a href="/wiki/Substitute_character" title="Substitute character">tofu</a> signs, due to its problem of font fallback mechanism, you may need the <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/advanced-font-settings/caclkomlalccbpcdllchkeecicepbmbm">Advanced Font Settings</a> extension to optimize. Renders Devanagari (used for Hindi), Bengali, Sinhala, Gurmukhi, and Tibetan scripts in the examples below, but not some of languages of Southeast Asian countries.</dd></dl>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Scripts">Scripts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Scripts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adlam">Adlam</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Adlam">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Adlam_script" title="Adlam script">Adlam</a> is a right-to-left alphabetic script devised by the brothers Ibrahima and Abdoulaye Barry, in order to represent the <a href="/wiki/Fula_language" title="Fula language">Fula language</a> (Fulani). It is supported by the following font:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website-2.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansAdlam-hinted.zip">Noto Sans Adlam (direct download link)</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansAdlam-Regular.ttf">(GitHub link)</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://unifoundry.com/unifont.html">Unifont Upper</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ebrima" title="Ebrima">Ebrima</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Update 1903 and later)</li></ul>

<tbody><tr>
<th>Correct rendering</th>
<th>Your browser/device
</th></tr>

</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Aegean_numerals">Aegean numerals</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Aegean numerals">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Aegean_numerals" title="Aegean numerals">Aegean numerals</a> were used by the <a href="/wiki/Minoan_civilization" title="Minoan civilization">Minoan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mycenaean_Greece" title="Mycenaean Greece">Mycenaean</a> civilizations.  They are supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://users.teilar.gr/~g1951d/">Aegean</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.evertype.com/emono/">Everson Mono</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://users.teilar.gr/~g1951d/">Symbola</a></li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ahom">Ahom</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Ahom">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Ahom_script" title="Ahom script">Ahom script</a> is a script used to write <a href="/wiki/Ahom_language" title="Ahom language">Ahom language</a>.  They are supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/tree/master/phaseIII_only/unhinted/ttf/NotoSerifAhom">Noto Serif Ahom</a>, a font made by Google.</li></ul>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th>Correct rendering</th>
<th>Your browser/device
</th></tr>
<tr>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ancient_South_Arabian">Ancient South Arabian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Ancient South Arabian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Ancient_South_Arabian_script" title="Ancient South Arabian script">Ancient South Arabian script</a> (Old South Arabian) was used to write the Minean, <a href="/wiki/Sabaean_language" title="Sabaean language">Sabaean</a>, <a href="/wiki/Qatabanian_language" title="Qatabanian language">Qatabanian</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hadramautic_language" title="Hadramautic language">Hadramite</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Himyaritic_language" title="Himyaritic language">Himyaritic</a> languages of <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a> from the 8th century BCE to the 6th century CE. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Everson_Mono" title="Everson Mono">Everson Mono</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website-2.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansOldSouthArabian-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Old South Arabian</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.alanwood.net/downloads/index.html#unicode">Qataban</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Quivira_(typeface)" title="Quivira (typeface)">Quivira</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Historic" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Historic</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 10 and later)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/GNU_Unifont" title="GNU Unifont">Unifont Upper</a></li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Armenian">Armenian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Armenian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/40px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="37" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/60px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/80px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://hy.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="hy:"> Armenian  edition</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a>, the free encyclopedia</td></tr>

<p>The <a href="/wiki/Armenian_alphabet" title="Armenian alphabet">Armenian alphabet</a> is only used to write the <a href="/wiki/Armenian_language" title="Armenian language">Armenian language</a>. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://dejavu-fonts.github.io/">DejaVu</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.gnu.org/software/freefont">GNU FreeSerif</a></li>

<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSerifArmenian-hinted.zip">Noto Serif Armenian (direct download link)</a>, the serif version of the font made by Google</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.deviantart.com/art/Kelvinch-Release-Version-600800030">Kelvinch Font</a></li>
<li>Segoe UI (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 7 and later, but only supports Armenian since Windows 8)</li>
<li>Sylfaen (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 2000 and later)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.hyeetch.nareg.com.au/armfont.html">Times LatArm</a></li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Balinese">Balinese</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Balinese">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/32px-Incubator-logo.svg.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="40" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/48px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/64px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="1000" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/ban" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/ban">Balinese test</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> at <a href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wikimedia_Incubator" class="extiw" title="meta:Wikimedia Incubator">Wikimedia Incubator</a></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Balinese_script" title="Balinese script">Balinese script</a> is used to write the <a href="/wiki/Balinese_language" title="Balinese language">Balinese language</a>. The script is encoded in <a href="/wiki/Unicode_block" title="Unicode block">block</a> "Balinese", code points 1B00–1B7F (<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.unicode.org/charts/PDF/U1B00.pdf">Unicode.org chart</a>). It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.alanwood.net/unicode/fonts-southeast-asian.html#balinese">Aksara Bali</a> (free <a href="/wiki/OpenType" title="OpenType">OpenType</a> font with keyboard driver)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansBalinese-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Balinese (direct download link)</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansBalinese-Regular.ttf">(GitHub link)</a>, a font made by Google</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bamum">Bamum</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Bamum">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Bamum_script" title="Bamum script">Bamum</a> is a series of scripts devised for the <a href="/wiki/Bamum_language" title="Bamum language">Bamum language</a> by <a href="/wiki/King_Njoya" class="mw-redirect" title="King Njoya">King Njoya</a> of <a href="/wiki/Cameroon" title="Cameroon">Cameroon</a> between 1896 and 1918. It is supported by the following font:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansBamum-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Bamum (direct download link)</a>, a font made by Google</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Batak">Batak</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Batak">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Batak_alphabet" class="mw-redirect" title="Batak alphabet">Batak alphabet</a> is used to write the <a href="/wiki/Batak_languages" title="Batak languages">Batak languages</a>. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>

<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansBatak-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Batak (direct download link)</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansBatak-Regular.ttf">(GitHub link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>

<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://sites.google.com/site/fontsundaprada/unduh-font-sunda-prada/prada.ttf">Prada (direct download link)</a></li></ul>

<h3><span id="Baybayin_.2F_Old_Tagalog"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Baybayin_/_Old_Tagalog">Baybayin / Old Tagalog</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Baybayin / Old Tagalog">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Baybayin" title="Baybayin">Baybayin</a> (also known as the <i>Tagalog script</i> in <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.unicode.org/charts/PDF/U1700.pdf">Unicode</a> and <i>Alibata</i>) is a form of pre-Spanish Philippine writing system from which modern minority scripts in the Philippines descended. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansTagalog-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Tagalog (direct download link)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansTagalog-Regular.ttf">(GitHub link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://paulmorrow.ca/fonts.htm">Paul Morrow's Baybayin Fonts</a>. Offers the most extensive list of Baybayin fonts for Windows and Macintosh operating systems</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.quivira-font.com">Quivira</a> is a proportional serif font that produces very readable text. Supports several scripts, among them the Baybayin script</li></ul>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th>Correct rendering</th>
<th>Your browser/device</th>
<th>Transliteration
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/File:Tagalog_in_Baybayin_script_postkudlit.png" class="image"><img alt="Tagalog in Baybayin script postkudlit.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Tagalog_in_Baybayin_script_postkudlit.png/400px-Tagalog_in_Baybayin_script_postkudlit.png" decoding="async" width="400" height="109" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Tagalog_in_Baybayin_script_postkudlit.png/600px-Tagalog_in_Baybayin_script_postkudlit.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/7/77/Tagalog_in_Baybayin_script_postkudlit.png 2x" data-file-width="787" data-file-height="214" /></a></td>
<td><span style="font-size: 16px;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r866778570">.mw-parser-output .script-baybayin{font-family:"Tagalog Doctrina 1593","Baybayin Lopez","Tagalog Stylized","Noto Sans Tagalog",Code2000}</style><span class="script-baybayin">ᜀᜅ᜔ ᜊᜏᜆ᜔ ᜆᜂ ᜀᜌ᜔ ᜁᜐᜒᜈᜒᜎᜅ᜔ ᜈ ᜋᜌ᜔ ᜃᜇᜉᜆᜈ᜔,<br />ᜀᜆ᜔ ᜉᜈ᜔ᜆᜌ᜔ ᜐ ᜇᜒᜄ᜔ᜈᜒᜇᜇ᜔,<br />ᜀᜆ᜔ ᜃᜇᜉᜆᜈ᜔ ᜀᜅ᜔ ᜆᜂ ᜀᜌ᜔ ᜊᜒᜈᜒᜌᜌᜀᜈ᜔ ᜅ᜔ ᜉᜄᜒᜁᜐᜒᜉ᜔,<br />ᜀᜆ᜔ ᜃᜇᜓᜈᜓᜅᜈ᜔ ᜈ ᜃᜁᜎᜅᜅ᜔ ᜋᜄ᜔ᜃᜁᜐ ᜐ ᜃᜉᜆᜒᜇᜈ᜔</span></span></td>
<td>Ang bawat tao ay isinilang na may karapatan, at pantay sa dignidad, at karapatan ang tao ay biniyayaan ng pag-iisip, at karapatan na kailangang magkaisa sa kapatiran.
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Note:</i> As of August 2018, this script is not being used on the <a href="https://tl.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="tl:">Tagalog Wikipedia</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Brahmi">Brahmi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Brahmi">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Brahmi_script" title="Brahmi script">Brahmi script</a> is one of the oldest writing systems used in <a href="/wiki/Ancient_India" class="mw-redirect" title="Ancient India">Ancient India</a> and present <a href="/wiki/South_Asia" title="South Asia">South</a> and <a href="/wiki/Central_Asia" title="Central Asia">Central Asia</a> from the 1st millennium BCE. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansBrahmi-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Brahmi (direct download link)</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansBrahmi-Regular.ttf">(GitHub link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Historic" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Historic</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 10 and later)</li></ul>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th>Correct rendering</th>
<th>Your browser/device
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/File:Brahmi_font_rendering_test.svg" class="image"><img alt="Brahmi font rendering test.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Brahmi_font_rendering_test.svg/88px-Brahmi_font_rendering_test.svg.png" decoding="async" width="88" height="22" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Brahmi_font_rendering_test.svg/132px-Brahmi_font_rendering_test.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Brahmi_font_rendering_test.svg/176px-Brahmi_font_rendering_test.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="224" data-file-height="55" /></a></td>
<td><span style="vertical-align:sub;"><span style="vertical-align:sub;line-height:180%"><span style="font-size:180%; vertical-align:sub;">𑀤𑁂𑀯𑀸𑀦𑀧𑀺𑀬𑁂𑀦</span></span></span>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Note:</i> The Brahmi script should not be confused with the family of <a href="/wiki/Brahmic_scripts" title="Brahmic scripts">Brahmic scripts</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Buhid">Buhid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Buhid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Buhid_alphabet" class="mw-redirect" title="Buhid alphabet">Buhid script</a> is used to write the <a href="/wiki/Buhid_language" title="Buhid language">Buhid language</a>. It is supported to varying extents by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansBuhid-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Buhid (direct download link)</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansBuhid-Regular.ttf">(GitHub link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><s><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.quivira-font.com">Quivira</a></s> <b>NOT RECOMMENDED FOR BUHID:</b> It contains basic Buhid letters but not the ligatures required to correctly render many Buhid syllables</li>
<li><s><a href="/wiki/Code2000" title="Code2000">Code2000</a></s> <b>NOT RECOMMENDED FOR BUHID:</b> It contains basic Buhid letters but not the ligatures required to correctly render many Buhid syllables</li></ul>

<tbody><tr>
<th>Correct rendering</th>
<th>Your browser/device</th>
<th>Sample syllables

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Burmese">Burmese</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Burmese">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main page: <a href="/wiki/Help:Multilingual_support_(Burmese)" title="Help:Multilingual support (Burmese)">Help:Multilingual support (Burmese)</a></div>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/40px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="37" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/60px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/80px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://my.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="my:"> Burmese  edition</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a>, the free encyclopedia</td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Burmese_alphabet" title="Burmese alphabet">Burmese alphabet</a> is used to write the <a href="/wiki/Burmese_language" title="Burmese language">Burmese language</a>. The script is encoded in block "Myanmar", code points 1000-109F (<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://unicode.org/charts/PDF/U1000.pdf">Unicode.org chart</a>). It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.myanmarnlp.net.mm/">Myanmar</a> (also available from <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/burmese/help/2010/02/000000_burmese_keyboard.shtml">BBCs website</a>)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.myanmarlanguage.org/article/download-unicode-fonts-and-keyboards">Myanmar Census</a></li>
<li>Myanmar Text (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 8 and later)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website-2.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansMyanmar-hinted.zip">Noto Sans Myanmar (direct download link)</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansMyanmar-Regular.ttf">(GitHub link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://scripts.sil.org/Padauk">Padauk</a> (supports <a href="/wiki/Graphite_(SIL)" title="Graphite (SIL)">Graphite</a>)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.myanmars.net/winmyanmar/">WinUni Innwa</a></li></ul>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th>Correct rendering</th>
<th>Your browser/device
</th></tr>
<tr>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Canadian_Aboriginal_Syllabics">Canadian Aboriginal Syllabics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Canadian Aboriginal Syllabics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/40px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="37" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/60px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/80px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://cr.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="cr:"> Cree  edition</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a>, the free encyclopedia</td></tr>
</tbody></table><table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/40px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="37" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/60px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/80px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://iu.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="iu:"> Inuktitut  edition</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a>, the free encyclopedia</td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p><a href="/wiki/Canadian_Aboriginal_syllabics" title="Canadian Aboriginal syllabics">Canadian Aboriginal syllabics</a> are an <a href="/wiki/Abugida" title="Abugida">abugida</a> used to write a number of <a href="/wiki/First_Nations" title="First Nations">First Nations</a> languages in Canada, including <a href="/wiki/Cree_language" title="Cree language">Cree</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ojibwe_language" title="Ojibwe language">Ojibwe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Naskapi" title="Naskapi">Naskapi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Inuktitut" title="Inuktitut">Inuktitut</a>, <a href="/wiki/Blackfoot_language" title="Blackfoot language">Blackfoot</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sayisi_Dene" title="Sayisi Dene">Sayisi</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Carrier_language" title="Carrier language">Carrier</a>. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li>Aboriginal Sans (<a href="/wiki/Help:Multilingual_support#Other_available_Unicode_fonts" title="Help:Multilingual support">See above</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Code2000" title="Code2000">Code2000</a> (<a href="/wiki/Help:Multilingual_support#Other_available_Unicode_fonts" title="Help:Multilingual support">See above</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Euphemia_(typeface)" title="Euphemia (typeface)">Euphemia</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows Vista and later)</li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Gadugi_(typeface)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Gadugi (typeface) (page does not exist)">Gadugi</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 10 Creators Update and later)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansCanadianAboriginal-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Canadian Aboriginal</a>, a font made by Google</li></ul>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th>Correct rendering</th>
<th>Your browser/device
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/File:Nehiyawewin.svg" class="image"><img alt="Nehiyawewin.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Nehiyawewin.svg/100px-Nehiyawewin.svg.png" decoding="async" width="100" height="19" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Nehiyawewin.svg/150px-Nehiyawewin.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/Nehiyawewin.svg/200px-Nehiyawewin.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="675" data-file-height="125" /></a></td>
<td style="font-size: 150%;">ᓀᐦᐃᔭᐍᐏᐣ
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Note:</i> As of August 2018, this script is not being used on the <a href="https://atj.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="atj:">Atikamekw Wikipedia</a>, plus <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/ojb" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/ojb">Ojibwe</a> and <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/bla" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/bla">Blackfoot</a> test wikis at the Wikimedia Incubator.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cham">Cham</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Cham">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cherokee">Cherokee</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Cherokee">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/40px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="37" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/60px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/80px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://chr.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="chr:"> Cherokee  edition</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a>, the free encyclopedia</td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Cherokee_syllabary" title="Cherokee syllabary">Cherokee syllabary</a>, used to write the <a href="/wiki/Cherokee_language" title="Cherokee language">Cherokee language</a>, is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.languagegeek.com/font/fontdownload.html">Cherokee Digohweli</a>, from LanguageGeek</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.gnu.org/software/freefont">GNU FreeFont</a></li>
<li>Gadugi (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 8 and later)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansCherokee-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Cherokee (direct download link)</a>, a font made by Google (Also supports lowercase)</li>
<li>Plantagenet Cherokee (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows Vista and later)</li></ul>
<p><a href="/wiki/Cherokee_syllabary#Unicode" title="Cherokee syllabary">Lowercase Cherokee</a> letters were added to Unicode version 8.0 in June, 2015. Font support for lowercase Cherokee is not yet widespread. Those fonts that do support lowercase are:
</p>
<ul><li>Gadugi (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 10 Creators Update and later)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansCherokee-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Cherokee (direct download link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://typeculture.com/foundry/font-collection/phoreus-cherokee/">Phoreus Cherokee</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.evertype.com/emono/">Everson Mono (beta version)</a></li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Coptic">Coptic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Coptic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/32px-Incubator-logo.svg.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="40" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/48px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/64px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="1000" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/cop" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/cop">Coptic test</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> at <a href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wikimedia_Incubator" class="extiw" title="meta:Wikimedia Incubator">Wikimedia Incubator</a></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Coptic_alphabet" title="Coptic alphabet">Coptic alphabet</a> is used to write the <a href="/wiki/Coptic_language" title="Coptic language">Coptic language</a>, which was used in Egypt before Arabic. It is currently used solely as a <a href="/wiki/Sacred_language" title="Sacred language">liturgical language</a>, and is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Alphabetum" title="Alphabetum">Alphabetum</a> is a commercial Unicode font, but it is the only font that provides Bohairic Coptic letters rather than Sahidic</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.gnu.org/software/freefont">GNU FreeSerif</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansCoptic-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Coptic (direct download link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.quivira-font.com/">Quivira</a>: Provides full Unicode support for all Coptic letters</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Historic" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Historic</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 10 and later)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Symbol" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Symbol</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 7 and later)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scripts.sil.org/SophiaNubian">Sophia Nubian</a> font by <a href="/wiki/SIL_International" title="SIL International">SIL International</a></li></ul>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th>Correct rendering</th>
<th>Your browser/device
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/File:Coptic-render.svg" class="image"><img alt="Coptic-render.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Coptic-render.svg/125px-Coptic-render.svg.png" decoding="async" width="125" height="17" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Coptic-render.svg/188px-Coptic-render.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Coptic-render.svg/250px-Coptic-render.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="447" data-file-height="62" /></a></td>
<td style="font-size: 180%;">ⲙⲛⲧⲣⲙⲛⲕⲏⲙⲉ
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cuneiform">Cuneiform</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Cuneiform">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/32px-Incubator-logo.svg.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="40" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/48px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/64px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="1000" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/sux" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/sux">Sumerian test</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> at <a href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wikimedia_Incubator" class="extiw" title="meta:Wikimedia Incubator">Wikimedia Incubator</a></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Cuneiform" title="Cuneiform">cuneiform script</a> was primarily used to write <a href="/wiki/Akkadian_language" title="Akkadian language">Akkadian</a> (including Assyrian and Babylonian) and <a href="/wiki/Sumerian_language" title="Sumerian language">Sumerian</a>. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="//noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansCuneiform-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Cuneiform (direct download link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Historic" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Historic</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 10 and later)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://oracc.museum.upenn.edu/doc/help/visitingoracc/fonts/index.html">Unicode Fonts for Oracc: Cuneiform Fonts</a> offers several different cuneiform fonts</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.hethport.uni-wuerzburg.de/cuneifont/">Unicode Cuneiform Fonts for Macintosh and Windows</a> offers cuneiform fonts as well</li></ul>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th>Correct rendering</th>
<th>Your browser/device
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/File:Cuneiform_Rendered.svg" class="image"><img alt="Cuneiform Rendered.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Cuneiform_Rendered.svg/150px-Cuneiform_Rendered.svg.png" decoding="async" width="150" height="24" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Cuneiform_Rendered.svg/225px-Cuneiform_Rendered.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Cuneiform_Rendered.svg/300px-Cuneiform_Rendered.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="801" data-file-height="127" /></a></td>
<td style="font-size: 150%;"><span style="font-size:125%;font-family:&#39;Segoe UI Historic&#39;,&#39;Akkadian&#39;,&#39;Noto Sans Cuneiform&#39;,&#39;Noto Sans Sumero-Akkadian Cuneiform&#39;;" title="cuneiform text" lang="und-Xsux">𒅎𒀝𒂵𒌈</span>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Deseret">Deseret</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Deseret">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Deseret_alphabet" title="Deseret alphabet">Deseret alphabet</a> is an alternative alphabet for writing the English language. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://copper.chem.ucla.edu/~jericks/Serif.html">"Bee" Serif fonts</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://copper.chem.ucla.edu/~jericks/Sans_Serif.html">"Bee" Sans Serif fonts</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansDeseret-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Deseret (direct download link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Symbol" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Symbol</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 7 and later)</li></ul>

</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Several Wikipedias use these scripts, including <a href="https://zh.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="zh:">Chinese</a>, <a href="https://zh-classical.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="zh-classical:">Classical Chinese</a>, <a href="https://zh-yue.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="zh-yue:">Cantonese</a> (Yue), <a href="https://gan.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="gan:">Gan</a>, <a href="https://ja.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="ja:">Japanese</a>, and <a href="https://ko.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="ko:">Korean</a>. They are not used (widely) in the <a href="https://zh-min-nan.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="zh-min-nan:">Min Nan</a>, <a href="https://za.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="za:">Zhuang</a>, or <a href="https://vi.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="vi:">Vietnamese</a> Wikipedias, even though the scripts are sometimes used in those languages, as well.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hentaigana">Hentaigana</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Hentaigana">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Hentaigana" title="Hentaigana">Hentaigana</a> are obsolete or nonstandard <a href="/wiki/Hiragana" title="Hiragana">hiragana</a> used occasionally on signage in <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>. Hentaigana characters are supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.babelstone.co.uk/Fonts/Han.html">BabelStone Han</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://osdn.net/projects/hanazono-font/releases/p12900">Hanazono Mincho</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://font.kim/#download">JIS Z 8903 Medium</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://wakufactory.jp/densho/font/hentai/">Unicode Hentaigana Font</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://osdn.net/projects/jis2004/wiki/FrontPage">WadaLabMaruGo2004Emoji and WadaLabChuMaruGo2004Emoji</a></li></ul>

<tbody><tr>
<th>Correct rendering</th>
<th>Your browser/device
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/File:Hiragana_NO_01.svg" class="image"><img alt="Hiragana NO 01.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Hiragana_NO_01.svg/30px-Hiragana_NO_01.svg.png" decoding="async" width="30" height="30" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Hiragana_NO_01.svg/45px-Hiragana_NO_01.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Hiragana_NO_01.svg/60px-Hiragana_NO_01.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="100" data-file-height="100" /></a></td>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Egyptian_Hieroglyphs">Egyptian Hieroglyphs</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Egyptian Hieroglyphs">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Egyptian_hieroglyphs" title="Egyptian hieroglyphs">Egyptian hieroglyphs</a> are supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://mjn.host.cs.st-andrews.ac.uk/egyptian/fonts/NewGardinerSMP.ttf">NewGardiner (direct download link)</a> (Recommended for better on-screen legibility)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansEgyptianHieroglyphs-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Egyptian Hieroglyphs (direct download link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Historic" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Historic</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 10 and later)</li></ul>
<p>Glyph stacking and formatting is accomplished via <a href="/wiki/Egyptian_Hieroglyph_Format_Controls" title="Egyptian Hieroglyph Format Controls">Egyptian Hieroglyph Format Controls</a>, which were added to version 12 of the <a href="/wiki/Unicode" title="Unicode">Unicode</a> standard in March 2019. However the above fonts do not yet support this feature.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Elbasan">Elbasan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Elbasan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Elbasan_script" title="Elbasan script">Elbasan script</a> is a mid 18th-century alphabetic script used for the <a href="/wiki/Albanian_language" title="Albanian language">Albanian language</a>. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlefonts/noto-fonts/blob/master/unhinted/NotoSansElbasan/NotoSansElbasan-Regular.ttf">Noto Sans Elbasan</a>, a font made by Google</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ethiopic">Ethiopic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Ethiopic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main page: <a href="/wiki/Help:Multilingual_support_(Ethiopic)" title="Help:Multilingual support (Ethiopic)">Help:Multilingual support (Ethiopic)</a></div>

</tbody></table><table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/40px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="37" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/60px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/80px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://ti.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="ti:"> Tigrinya  edition</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a>, the free encyclopedia</td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Ethiopic_syllabary" class="mw-redirect" title="Ethiopic syllabary">Ethiopic syllabary</a> is used in central <a href="/wiki/East_Africa" title="East Africa">east Africa</a> for <a href="/wiki/Amharic" title="Amharic">Amharic</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bilen_language" title="Bilen language">Bilen</a>, <a href="/wiki/Oromo_language" title="Oromo language">Oromo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tigre_language" title="Tigre language">Tigre</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tigrinya_language" title="Tigrinya language">Tigrinya</a>, and other languages. It evolved from the script for classical <a href="/wiki/Ge%27ez" class="mw-redirect" title="Ge&#39;ez">Ge'ez</a>, which is now strictly a <a href="/wiki/Liturgical_language" class="mw-redirect" title="Liturgical language">liturgical language</a>. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://scripts.sil.org/AbyssinicaSIL">Abyssinica SIL</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.senamirmir.com/projects/typography/typeface.html">Ethiopia Jiret</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.evertype.com/emono/">Everson Mono</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansEthiopic-hinted.zip">Noto Sans Ethiopic (direct download link)</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansEthiopic-Regular.ttf">(GitHub link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nyala_(typeface)" title="Nyala (typeface)">Nyala</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows Vista and later)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://titus.fkidg1.uni-frankfurt.de/unicode/tmp/tmp1/tu91503.zip">TITUS Cyberbit (direct download link)</a></li></ul>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th>Correct rendering</th>
<th>Your browser/device
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/File:Ethiopiya-text.svg" class="image"><img alt="Ethiopiya-text.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Ethiopiya-text.svg/100px-Ethiopiya-text.svg.png" decoding="async" width="100" height="26" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Ethiopiya-text.svg/150px-Ethiopiya-text.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Ethiopiya-text.svg/200px-Ethiopiya-text.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="548" data-file-height="140" /></a></td>
<td style="font-size: 200%;">ኢትዮጵያ
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Note:</i> As of August 2018, this script is not being used on the <a href="https://om.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="om:">Oromo Wikipedia</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gothic">Gothic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Gothic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/40px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="37" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/60px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/80px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://got.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="got:"> Gothic  edition</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a>, the free encyclopedia</td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Gothic_alphabet" title="Gothic alphabet">Gothic alphabet</a>, which is used to write the <a href="/wiki/Gothic_language" title="Gothic language">Gothic language</a>, is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.scholarsfonts.net/cardofnt.html">Cardo</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.wazu.jp/gallery/views/View_MPH2BDamase.html">MPH 2B Damase</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://junicode.sourceforge.net/">Junicode</a>, a free font mostly for Medieval scripts.</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansGothic-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Gothic (direct download link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li>Robert Pfeffer’s fonts: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://robert-pfeffer.net/schriftarten/midjungards.html"><cite>Midjungards</cite></a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://robert-pfeffer.net/schriftarten/pfeffer_mediaeval_gotisch.html"><cite>Pfeffer Mediæval</cite></a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://robert-pfeffer.net/schriftarten/silubr.html"><cite>Silubr</cite></a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://robert-pfeffer.net/schriftarten/skeirs.html"><cite>Skeirs</cite></a>, and <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://robert-pfeffer.net/schriftarten/ulfilas.html"><cite>Ulfilas</cite></a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Historic" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Historic</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 10 and later)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Symbol" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Symbol</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 7 and later)</li></ul>

<h3><span id="Hanun.C3.B3.27o"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Hanunó'o">Hanunó'o</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Hanunó&#039;o">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Hanun%C3%B3%27o_alphabet" class="mw-redirect" title="Hanunó&#39;o alphabet">Hanunó'o script</a> is used to write the <a href="/wiki/Hanun%C3%B3%27o_language" class="mw-redirect" title="Hanunó&#39;o language">Hanunó'o language</a>. It is supported to varying extents by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.gnu.org/software/freefont">GNU FreeFont</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansHanunoo-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Hanunoo (direct download link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><s><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.quivira-font.com">Quivira</a></s> <b>NOT RECOMMENDED FOR HANUNÓ'O:</b> It contains basic Hanunó'o letters but not the ligatures required to correctly render many Hanunó'o syllables</li></ul>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th>Correct rendering</th>
<th>Your browser/device</th>
<th>Sample syllables
</th></tr>

<td style="font-family:&#39;Noto Sans Hanunoo&#39;, Quivira;"><span style="vertical-align:sub;"><span style="vertical-align:sub;line-height:180%"><span style="font-size:180%; vertical-align:sub;">ᜥᜥᜲᜥᜳ</span></span></span></td>

<td>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>These scripts are used in a great many Wikipedias, including the ones for <a href="https://as.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="as:">Assamese</a>, <a href="https://bn.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="bn:">Bengali</a>, <a href="https://bh.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="bh:">Bhojpuri</a>, <a href="https://bpy.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="bpy:">Bishnupriya Manipuri</a>, <a href="https://bo.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="bo:">Central Tibetan</a>, <a href="https://dz.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="dz:">Dzongkha</a>, <a href="https://gu.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="gu:">Gujarati</a>, <a href="https://kn.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="kn:">Kannada</a>, <a href="https://ks.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="ks:">Kashmiri</a>, <a href="https://gom.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="gom:">Goan Konkani</a>, <a href="https://mai.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="mai:">Maithili</a>, <a href="https://ml.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="ml:">Malayalam</a>, <a href="https://mr.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="mr:">Marathi</a>, <a href="https://ne.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="ne:">Nepali</a>, <a href="https://new.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="new:">Newar</a>, <a href="https://or.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="or:">Odia</a>, <a href="https://pi.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="pi:">Pali</a>, <a href="https://pa.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="pa:">Eastern Punjabi</a>, <a href="https://sa.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="sa:">Sanskrit</a>, <a href="https://si.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="si:">Sinhalese</a>, <a href="https://ta.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="ta:">Tamil</a>, <a href="https://te.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="te:">Telugu</a>, and <a href="https://tcy.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="tcy:">Tulu</a>.
</p><p>They are also used in the Wikimedia Incubator test wikis for <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/anp" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/anp">Angika</a>, <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/awa" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/awa">Awadhi</a>, <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/bfq" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/bfq">Badaga</a>, <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/brx" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/brx">Bodo</a>, <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/hne" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/hne">Chhattisgarhi</a>, <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/bgc" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/bgc">Haryanvi</a>, <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/kev" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/kev">Kanikkaran</a>, <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/kfr" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/kfr">Kutchi</a>, <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/raj" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/raj">Rajasthani</a>, <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/saz" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/saz">Saurashtra</a>, and <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/taj" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/taj">Tamang</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Inscriptional_Parthian">Inscriptional Parthian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Inscriptional Parthian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Inscriptional_Parthian" title="Inscriptional Parthian">Inscriptional Parthian</a> was used for writing the <a href="/wiki/Parthian_language" title="Parthian language">Parthian language</a>. It is supported by the following fonts:

<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Historic" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Historic</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 10 and later)</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Javanese">Javanese</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Javanese">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/40px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="37" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/60px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/80px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://jv.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="jv:"> Javanese  edition</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a>, the free encyclopedia</td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Javanese_script" title="Javanese script">Javanese script</a> is used to write the <a href="/wiki/Javanese_language" title="Javanese language">Javanese language</a>. It is supported by Unicode 5.2 and above. The script is a so-called <i>SIL Graphite</i>-script, and is best supported by Firefox. As of recently however, it can be rendered by the OpenType and TrueType standards, provided the right font is used. The script is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansJavanese-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Javanese (direct download link)</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansJavanese-Regular.ttf">(GitHub link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li>Javanese Text (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 8.1 and later)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://sites.google.com/site/jawaunicode/download/">Tuladha Jejeg</a>, a free SIL Graphite font</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://sites.google.com/site/fontsundaprada/unduh-font-sunda-prada/prada.ttf">Prada (direct download link)</a></li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kaithi">Kaithi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Kaithi">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Kaithi" title="Kaithi">Kaithi</a>, also called "Kayathi" or "Kayasthi", is a historical script used widely in parts of <a href="/wiki/North_India" title="North India">North India</a>.  It is supported by the following font:

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kharosthi">Kharosthi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Kharosthi">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b><a href="/wiki/Kharosthi" title="Kharosthi">Kharosthi</a></b>, also spelled <b>Kharoshthi</b> or <b>Kharoṣṭhī</b>, is an ancient script used in <a href="/wiki/Gandhara" title="Gandhara">ancient Gandhara</a> and <a href="/wiki/Outline_of_ancient_India" title="Outline of ancient India">ancient India</a>.
It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><s><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlefonts/noto-fonts/blob/master/unhinted/NotoSansKharoshthi/NotoSansKharoshthi-Regular.ttf">Noto Sans Kharosthi</a> </s> <b> NOT RECOMMENDED:</b> Even though it’s a font made by Google, it doesn’t render many necessary conjunctions, but Segoe UI does. It also has misplaced vowel marks.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Historic" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Historic</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 10 and later)</li></ul>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th>Correct rendering</th>
<th>Your browser/device

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Khudabadi">Khudabadi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Khudabadi">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><b><a href="/wiki/Khudabadi" class="mw-redirect" title="Khudabadi">Khudabadi</a></b>, also spelled <b>Khudawadi</b>, or <b>Sindhi</b>, is a script used to write <a href="/wiki/Sindhi_Language" class="mw-redirect" title="Sindhi Language">Sindhi Language</a>.

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Klingon">Klingon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Klingon">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Klingon_script" class="mw-redirect" title="Klingon script">Klingon script</a> is used to write the <a href="/wiki/Klingon_language" title="Klingon language">Klingon language</a>, an artistic language of the <i><a href="/wiki/Star_Trek" title="Star Trek">Star Trek</a></i> franchise. The script is not encoded in <a href="/wiki/Unicode" title="Unicode">Unicode</a> but a range of code points defined in the <a href="/wiki/ConScript_Unicode_Registry" title="ConScript Unicode Registry">ConScript Unicode Registry</a> (CSUR) is in common use. The following fonts support these CSUR code points:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Code2000" title="Code2000">Code2000</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Unifont_CSUR" class="mw-redirect" title="Unifont CSUR">Unifont CSUR</a> (A part of GNU Unifont, which only supports glyphs in <a href="/wiki/ConScript_Unicode_Registry" title="ConScript Unicode Registry">CSUR</a>)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.kreativekorp.com/software/fonts/constructium.shtml">Constructium</a></li></ul>

<tbody><tr>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Linear_A">Linear A</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Linear A">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The undeciphered <a href="/wiki/Linear_A" title="Linear A">Linear A</a> script was used in <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Greece" title="Ancient Greece">ancient Greece</a>. It is supported by the following fonts:

<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://users.teilar.gr/~g1951d/">Aegean</a></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Linear_B">Linear B</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Linear B">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Linear_B" title="Linear B">Linear B</a> script was used for writing <a href="/wiki/Mycenaean_Greek" title="Mycenaean Greek">Mycenaean Greek</a>, the earliest attested form of the <a href="/wiki/Greek_language" title="Greek language">Greek language</a>. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website-2.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansLinearB-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Linear B (direct download link)</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansLinearB-Regular.ttf">(GitHub link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.evertype.com/emono/">Everson Mono</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/GNU_Unifont" title="GNU Unifont">Unifont Upper</a></li></ul>

<th>Your browser/device

<td style="font-size:300%;">𐁂𐀐𐀷

<h3><span id="Lisu_.28Fraser_alphabet.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Lisu_(Fraser_alphabet)">Lisu (Fraser alphabet)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Lisu (Fraser alphabet)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Fraser_alphabet" class="mw-redirect" title="Fraser alphabet">Fraser alphabet</a> is used only to write the <a href="/wiki/Lisu_language" title="Lisu language">Lisu language</a>. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://dejavu-fonts.github.io/">DejaVu</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://phjamr.github.io/miao.html#install">Miao Unicode</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansLisu-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Lisu (direct download link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li>Segoe UI (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 7 and later, but only supports Lisu since Windows 8)</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lontara">Lontara</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Lontara">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/40px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="37" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/60px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/80px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://bug.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="bug:"> Buginese  edition</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a>, the free encyclopedia</td></tr>

<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/32px-Incubator-logo.svg.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="40" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/48px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/64px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="1000" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/mak" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/mak">Makassarese test</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> at <a href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wikimedia_Incubator" class="extiw" title="meta:Wikimedia Incubator">Wikimedia Incubator</a></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Lontara_script" title="Lontara script">Lontara script</a> is used to write <a href="/wiki/Buginese_language" title="Buginese language">Buginese</a>, <a href="/wiki/Makassarese_language" title="Makassarese language">Makassarese</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Mandar_language" title="Mandar language">Mandar</a>. The script is encoded in <a href="/wiki/Unicode_block" title="Unicode block">block</a> "Buginese", code points 1A00–1A1F (<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.unicode.org/charts/PDF/U1A00.pdf">Unicode.org chart</a>). It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li>Leelawadee UI, note that Leelawadee does <b>not</b> support the Lontara script, only the <i>UI</i> version does. Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 8 and later</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.alanwood.net/downloads/mph-2b-damase.zip">MPH 2B Damase (direct download link)</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website-2.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansBuginese-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Buginese (direct download link)</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansBuginese-Regular.ttf">(GitHub link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://niariot87.googlepages.com/">Saweri</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://sites.google.com/site/fontsundaprada/unduh-font-sunda-prada/prada.ttf">Prada (direct download link)</a></li></ul>
