<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Mongolian">Mongolian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Mongolian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/32px-Incubator-logo.svg.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="40" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/48px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/64px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="1000" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/mvf" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/mvf">Peripheral Mongolian test</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> at <a href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wikimedia_Incubator" class="extiw" title="meta:Wikimedia Incubator">Wikimedia Incubator</a></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Mongolian_script" title="Mongolian script">Mongolian script</a> is occasionally used to write the <a href="/wiki/Mongolian_language" title="Mongolian language">Mongolian language</a> on the internet, though <a href="/wiki/Cyrillic_script" title="Cyrillic script">Cyrillic</a> is more common. It is also used to write the <a href="/wiki/Manchu_language" title="Manchu language">Manchu language</a> and <a href="/wiki/Xibe_language" title="Xibe language">Xibe language</a>. It is written from top to bottom in columns ordered from left to right. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansMongolian-unhinted.zip#http://fonts.gstatic.com/ea/notosansmongolian/v1/download.zip">Noto Sans Mongolian (direct download link)</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansMongolian-Regular.ttf">(GitHub link)</a>, a font made by Google, but only supports horizontal rendering in some bad rendering device such as Apple.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Code2000" title="Code2000">Code2000</a></li>
<li>Oyun font series by Inner Mongolian University: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://oyun.mglip.com/mongolfont/download_font.aspx?fid=1">Oyun Qagan Tig</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://oyun.mglip.com/mongolfont/download_font.aspx?fid=2">Oyun Garqag Tig</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://oyun.mglip.com/mongolfont/download_font.aspx?fid=3">Oyun Hawang Tig</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://oyun.mglip.com/mongolfont/download_font.aspx?fid=4">Oyun Scnin Tig</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://oyun.mglip.com/mongolfont/download_font.aspx?fid=5">Oyun Gar Biqimel Tig</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://oyun.mglip.com/mongolfont/download_font.aspx?fid=6">Oyun Har_a Tig</a>, and <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://oyun.mglip.com/mongolfont/download_font.aspx?fid=7">Oyun Gurban Ulus Tig</a></li>
<li>Menksoft font series: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.menksoft.com//Portals//_MenkCms//Products//Fonts//MenksoftOpenType1.02//MQG8F02.ttf">Menk Qagan Tig</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.menksoft.com//Portals//_MenkCms//Products//Fonts//MenksoftOpenType1.02//MGQ8102.ttf">Menk Garqag Tig</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.menksoft.com//Portals//_MenkCms//Products//Fonts//MenksoftOpenType1.02//MHR8102.ttf">Menk Har_a Tig</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.menksoft.com//Portals//_MenkCms//Products//Fonts//MenksoftOpenType1.02//MHW8102.ttf">Menk Hawang Tig</a>, and <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.menksoft.com//Portals//_MenkCms//Products//Fonts//MenksoftOpenType1.02//MSN8102.ttf">Menk Scnin Tig</a></li>
<li>Mongolian Baiti (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 7 and later)</li>
<li>Mongol Usug</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://hkuri.cneas.tohoku.ac.jp/project2/font">Mongolian Universal White</a> (free font)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://mongolfont.com/en/font/mnglwhiteotf.html">Mongolian White</a> (free font)</li>
<li>MongolianScript</li></ul>

<th>Correct rendering</th>

</th></tr>
<tr>
<td align="center"><a href="/wiki/File:Monggol_bicig.svg" class="image"><img alt="Monggol bicig.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Monggol_bicig.svg/35px-Monggol_bicig.svg.png" decoding="async" width="35" height="120" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Monggol_bicig.svg/52px-Monggol_bicig.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Monggol_bicig.svg/70px-Monggol_bicig.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="140" data-file-height="480" /></a></td>
<td style="font-size: 200%;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r886223191">.mw-parser-output .font-mong{font-family:"Menk Hawang Tig","Menk Qagan Tig","Menk Garqag Tig","Menk Har_a Tig","Menk Scnin Tig","Oyun Gurban Ulus Tig","Oyun Qagan Tig","Oyun Garqag Tig","Oyun Har_a Tig","Oyun Scnin Tig","Oyun Agula Tig","Mongolian Baiti","Noto Sans Mongolian","Mongolian Universal White","Mongol Usug","Mongolian White","MongolianScript","Code2000","Menksoft Qagan"}.mw-parser-output .font-mong-mnc,.mw-parser-output .font-mong:lang(mnc-Mong),.mw-parser-output .font-mong:lang(dta-Mong),.mw-parser-output .font-mong:lang(sjo-Mong){font-family:"Abkai Xanyan","Abkai Xanyan LA","Abkai Xanyan VT","Abkai Xanyan XX","Abkai Xanyan SC","Abkai Buleku","Daicing White","Mongolian Baiti","Noto Sans Mongolian","Mongolian Universal White"}</style><span lang="mn-Mong" class="font-mong" style="display:inline-block; font-weight:normal; font-size: 1.25em; line-height: 1.25em; -webkit-writing-mode: vertical-lr; -o-writing-mode: vertical-lr; -ms-writing-mode: tb-lr; writing-mode: tb-lr; writing-mode: vertical-lr; vertical-align:text-top;"><span class="nowrap">ᠮᠣᠩᠭᠣᠯ ᠪᠢᠴᠢᠭ᠌</span></span>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><i>Note:</i> As of August 2018, this script is not being generally used on the <a href="https://mn.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="mn:">Mongolian Wikipedia</a> (which uses Cyrillic in general).
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="New_Tai_Lue">New Tai Lue</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: New Tai Lue">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/32px-Incubator-logo.svg.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="40" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/48px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/64px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="1000" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/khb" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/khb">Tai Lue test</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> at <a href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wikimedia_Incubator" class="extiw" title="meta:Wikimedia Incubator">Wikimedia Incubator</a></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p><a href="/wiki/New_Tai_Lue_alphabet" title="New Tai Lue alphabet">New Tai Lue script</a>, also known as Simplified Tai Lue, is used to write the <a href="/wiki/Tai_Lue_language" title="Tai Lue language">Tai Lue language</a> (Tai Lü).
It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scripts.sil.org/SILFontList">Dai Banna SIL fonts</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_typefaces_included_with_Microsoft_Windows" title="List of typefaces included with Microsoft Windows">Microsoft New Tai Lue</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website-2.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansNewTaiLue-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans New Tai Lue</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansNewTaiLue-Regular.ttf">(GitHub link)</a></li></ul>

<h3><span id="N.C3.BCshu"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Nüshu">Nüshu</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Nüshu">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/N%C3%BCshu" title="Nüshu">Nüshu</a> is a syllabic script derived from Chinese characters that was used exclusively among women in <a href="/wiki/Jiangyong_County" title="Jiangyong County">Jiangyong County</a> in <a href="/wiki/Hunan" title="Hunan">Hunan</a> province of southern <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a>. It is supported by the following font:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://yedict.com/download/">TH-Tshyn-P1, TH-Feon-B</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://unifoundry.com/unifont.html">Unifont Upper</a></li></ul>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th>Correct rendering</th>
<th>Your browser/device
</th></tr>

</td></tr></tbody></table>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Nyiakeng_Puachue_Hmong">Nyiakeng Puachue Hmong</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Nyiakeng Puachue Hmong">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Nyiakeng_Puachue_Hmong" title="Nyiakeng Puachue Hmong">Nyiakeng Puachue Hmong</a> is an alphabet script devised for <a href="/wiki/Hmong_language" title="Hmong language">White Hmong and Green Hmong</a> in the 1980s by Reverend Chervang Kong for use within his United Christians Liberty Evangelical Church. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://unifoundry.com/unifont.html">Unifont Upper</a></li></ul>
<table class="wikitable">

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ogham">Ogham</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Ogham">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Ogham" title="Ogham">Ogham</a> alphabet was used to write the <a href="/wiki/Old_Irish_language" class="mw-redirect" title="Old Irish language">Old Irish language</a> from the 1st to 9th century AD. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://babelstone.co.uk/Fonts/Ogham.html">BabelStone Ogham Fonts</a>, a series of free fonts for Ogham made by <a href="/wiki/Andrew_West_(linguist)" title="Andrew West (linguist)">Andrew West</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://dejavu-fonts.github.io/">DejaVu</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.evertype.com/emono/">Everson Mono</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansOgham-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Ogham (direct download link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Historic" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Historic</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 10 and later)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Symbol" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Symbol</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 7 and later)</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ol_Chiki">Ol Chiki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Ol Chiki">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/40px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="37" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/60px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/80px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://sat.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="sat:"> Santali  edition</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a>, the free encyclopedia</td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Ol_Chiki_script" title="Ol Chiki script">Ol Chiki script</a> script was created in 1925 by <a href="/wiki/Raghunath_Murmu" title="Raghunath Murmu">Raghunath Murmu</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Santali_language" title="Santali language">Santali language</a>.
It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Code2000" title="Code2000">Code2000</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nirmala_UI" title="Nirmala UI">Nirmala UI</a> (regular and semilight)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://santaliwiki.blogspot.com/p/download-santali-ol-chiki-fonts.html">OLCK UNI22nd Dec03 &amp; OLCK UNI Raghunath Murmu</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.google.com/get/noto/#sans-olck">Noto Sans Ol Chiki</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://cdac.in/index.aspx?id=dl_sakal_bharati_font">Sakal Bharati</a></li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Project_Ol_chiki">Guru Gomke font</a> - <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/GuruGomke/files/raw/master/Font%20files/download-fonts.zip">Guru Gomke font download</a></li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Old_Persian_cuneiform">Old Persian cuneiform</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: Old Persian cuneiform">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Old_Persian_cuneiform" title="Old Persian cuneiform">Old Persian cuneiform</a> script was used to write the <a href="/wiki/Old_Persian_language" class="mw-redirect" title="Old Persian language">Old Persian language</a>. The script is encoded in <a href="/wiki/Unicode_block" title="Unicode block">block</a> "Old Persian", code points 103A0–103DF (<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.unicode.org/charts/PDF/U103A0.pdf">Unicode.org chart</a>). It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://users.teilar.gr/~g1951d/">Aegean</a> (free font)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansOldPersian-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Old Persian (direct download link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Historic" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Historic</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 10 and later)</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Osage">Osage</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: Osage">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Osage_alphabet" class="mw-redirect" title="Osage alphabet">Osage alphabet</a> is used to write <a href="/wiki/Osage_language" title="Osage language">Osage</a>, a Native American language spoken in <a href="/wiki/Oklahoma" title="Oklahoma">Oklahoma</a>. <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Phaistos_Disc">Phaistos Disc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Phaistos Disc">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Psalter_Pahlavi">Psalter Pahlavi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: Psalter Pahlavi">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Psalter_Pahlavi" title="Psalter Pahlavi">Psalter Pahlavi</a> was used for writing <a href="/wiki/Middle_Persian" title="Middle Persian">Middle Persian</a> on paper.  It is supported by the following font:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansPsalterPahlavi-Regular.ttf">Noto Sans Psalter Pahlavi</a>, a font made by google</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Historic" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Historic</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 10 and later)</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Runes">Runes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Runes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Runes" title="Runes">Runes</a> are supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://babelstone.co.uk/Fonts/AngloSaxon.html">BabelStone Anglo-Saxon Runic fonts</a>, a series of free font for Runes that are used in Frisian and Anglo-Saxon inscriptions from the 5th to 11th centuries, made by <a href="/wiki/Andrew_West_(linguist)" title="Andrew West (linguist)">Andrew West</a>.</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://junicode.sourceforge.net/">Junicode</a>, a free font mostly for Medieval scripts</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansRunic-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Runic (direct download link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Historic" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Historic</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 10 and later)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Symbol" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Symbol</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 7 and later)</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sharada">Sharada</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Sharada">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Sharada_script" title="Sharada script">Sharada script</a> is a Brahmic script that is almost extinct. It is used (rarely) to write the <a href="/wiki/Kashmiri_language" title="Kashmiri language">Kashmiri language</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sanskrit" title="Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a>. It's available in those fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansSharada-Regular.ttf">Noto Sans Sharada</a>, a font made by Google</li></ul>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th>Correct rendering</th>
<th>Your browser/device</th>
<th>Transliteration
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/File:Koshur_in_Sharada_Script.png" class="image"><img alt="Koshur in Sharada Script.png" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Koshur_in_Sharada_Script.png/50px-Koshur_in_Sharada_Script.png" decoding="async" width="50" height="29" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Koshur_in_Sharada_Script.png/75px-Koshur_in_Sharada_Script.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Koshur_in_Sharada_Script.png/100px-Koshur_in_Sharada_Script.png 2x" data-file-width="123" data-file-height="72" /></a></td>

<td>Koshur
</td></tr></tbody></table>

</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Siddham">Siddham</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: Siddham">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sora_Sompeng">Sora Sompeng</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: Sora Sompeng">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Sora_Sompeng" class="mw-redirect" title="Sora Sompeng">Sora Sompeng</a> Alphabet is a Brahmic Script, which is a script to write <a href="/wiki/Sora_language" title="Sora language">Sora language</a>, a language spoken by about 300,000 people. It is available in these fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansSoraSompeng-Regular.ttf">Noto Sans Sora Sompeng</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nirmala_UI" title="Nirmala UI">Nirmala UI</a></li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sundanese">Sundanese</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=63" title="Edit section: Sundanese">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/40px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="37" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/60px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/80px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://su.wikipedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="su:"> Sundanese  edition</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a>, the free encyclopedia</td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Sundanese_script" title="Sundanese script">Sundanese script</a> is used to write the <a href="/wiki/Sundanese_language" title="Sundanese language">Sundanese language</a>. The script is encoded in <a href="/wiki/Unicode_block" title="Unicode block">block</a> "Sundanese", code points 1B80–1BBF (<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.unicode.org/charts/PDF/U1B80.pdf">Unicode.org chart</a>). It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansSundanese-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Sundanese (direct download link)</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansSundanese-Regular.ttf">(GitHub link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.kairaga.com/download/sundanese-unicode-2-0-ttf?wpdmdl=3083&amp;refresh=5db92a9961fe01572416153">Sundanese Unicode (direct download link)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.kairaga.com/download/sundanese-unicode-2-0-ttf">main download page</a> (free font)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://sites.google.com/site/fontsundaprada/unduh-font-sunda-prada/prada.ttf">Prada (direct download link)</a></li></ul>
<table class="wikitable">
<tbody><tr>
<th>Correct rendering</th>
<th>Your browser/device</th>
<th>Transliteration
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/File:Ladrang-sunda.svg" class="image"><img alt="Ladrang-sunda.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Ladrang-sunda.svg/250px-Ladrang-sunda.svg.png" decoding="async" width="250" height="225" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Ladrang-sunda.svg/375px-Ladrang-sunda.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Ladrang-sunda.svg/500px-Ladrang-sunda.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="2041" data-file-height="1840" /></a></td>
<td><span lang="su" style="font-family:&#39;Sundanese Unicode&#39;,&#39;Noto Sans Sundanese&#39;; font-size:;"><span style="vertical-align:sub;"><span style="vertical-align:sub;line-height:180%"><span style="font-size:180%; vertical-align:sub;">&#x1b9c;ᮓᮢᮀ<br />ᮃᮚ ᮠᮤᮏᮤ ᮛᮥᮕ ᮞᮒᮧ ᮜᮩᮒᮤᮊ᮪,<br />ᮆᮀᮊᮀ-ᮆᮀᮊᮀ, ᮆᮀᮊᮀ-ᮆᮀᮊᮀ,<br />ᮞᮧᮊ᮪ ᮜᮥᮜᮥᮙ᮪ᮎᮒᮔ᮪ ᮓᮤ ᮎᮄ,<br />ᮃᮛᮤ ᮘᮍᮥᮔ᮪ ᮃᮛᮦᮊ᮪ ᮞᮛᮥᮕ ᮏᮀ<br />ᮜᮔ᮪ᮎᮂ.</span></span></span></span></td>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sutton_SignWriting">Sutton SignWriting</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=64" title="Edit section: Sutton SignWriting">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Sutton_SignWriting" class="mw-redirect" title="Sutton SignWriting">Sutton SignWriting</a> is used to write any <a href="/wiki/Sign_language" title="Sign language">Sign language</a>. It is supported with the SignWriting 2010 Typeface which includes 2 TrueType fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/Slevinski/signwriting_2010_fonts">SignWriting 2010 Fonts project on GitHub</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/Slevinski/signwriting_2010_fonts@master/fonts/SignWriting%202010.ttf">SignWriting 2010 TrueType Font</a> and <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/Slevinski/signwriting_2010_fonts@master/fonts/SignWriting%202010%20Filling.ttf">SignWriting 2010 Filling TrueType Font</a> (direct downloads)</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sylheti_Nagari">Sylheti Nagari</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=65" title="Edit section: Sylheti Nagari">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Sylheti Nagari (Silôṭi Nagri) is an endangered script used for writing <a href="/wiki/Sylheti_language" title="Sylheti language">Sylheti language</a>. It's available in those fonts:

<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/tree/master/phaseIII_only/unhinted/ttf/">Noto Sans Siloti Nagari</a>, a font made by Google</li></ul>

<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/32px-Incubator-logo.svg.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="40" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/48px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/64px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="1000" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/aii" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/aii">Assyrian Neo-Aramaic test</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> at <a href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wikimedia_Incubator" class="extiw" title="meta:Wikimedia Incubator">Wikimedia Incubator</a></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Syriac_alphabet" title="Syriac alphabet">Syriac</a> and <a href="/wiki/Aramaic_alphabet" title="Aramaic alphabet">Aramaic</a> scripts are used to write the <a href="/wiki/Syriac_language" title="Syriac language">Syriac</a> and <a href="/wiki/Aramaic_language" class="mw-redirect" title="Aramaic language">Aramaic</a> languages. As with most <a href="/wiki/Semitic" class="mw-disambig" title="Semitic">Semitic</a> scripts, these scripts flow from right to left, which can cause letters to appear in the wrong order on some left-to-right systems. The tag &#123;&#123;<a href="/wiki/Template:Rtl-lang" title="Template:Rtl-lang">rtl-lang</a>&#125;&#125; can fix this issue.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources.">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>Most operating systems provide support for Syriac scripts natively, but only the <i>Maḏnḥāyā</i> (<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r914935762">.mw-parser-output .script-Syre{font-family:"Estrangelo Antioch","Estrangelo Edessa","Estrangelo Midyat","Estrangelo Nisibin","Estrangelo Quenneshrin","Estrangelo Talada","Estrangelo TurAbdin","Noto Sans Syriac","Noto Sans Syriac Estrangela","Segoe UI Historic"}.mw-parser-output .script-Syrj{font-family:"Serto Batnan","Serto Jerusalem","Serto Kharput","Serto Malankara","Serto Mardin","Serto Urhoy","Noto Sans Syriac","Noto Sans Syriac Western"}.mw-parser-output .script-Syrn{font-family:"East Syriac Adiabene","East Syriac Ctesiphon","Noto Sans Syriac","Noto Sans Syriac Eastern",FreeSans,Code2000}</style><span class="script-Syrn" dir="rtl" style="font-size:125%;" lang="syc-Syrn">ܡܕܢܚܝܐ</span>&#8206;) and <i>ʾEsṭrangēlā</i> (<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r914935762"/><span class="script-Syre" dir="rtl" style="font-size: 125%;" lang="syc-Syre">ܐܣܛܪܢܓܠܐ</span>&#8206;) varieties have correct rendering.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;c&#93;</a></sup> In order to render the <i>Serṭā</i> (<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r914935762"/><span class="script-Syrj" dir="rtl" style="font-size:125%;" lang="syc-Syrj">ܣܪܛܐ</span>&#8206;) variety, additional fonts are needed. These scripts are supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><s><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.atour.com/fonts/">Aramaic Fonts</a></s> <b>NOT RECOMMENDED FOR SYRIAC:</b> It uses code points from other languages and thus will cause other languages to render incorrectly</li>
<li>Estrangelo Edessa (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows XP and later)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Segoe#Segoe_UI_Historic" title="Segoe">Segoe UI Historic</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 10 and later)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.bethmardutho.org/meltho/">Meltho OpenType™ Syriac Fonts</a> (free font)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansSyriacEastern-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Syraic Eastern</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansSyriacEstrangela-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Syriac Estrangela</a>, and <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansSyriacWestern-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Syriac Western</a> (direct download links). <a href="/wiki/Noto_fonts" title="Noto fonts">Noto fonts</a> made by Google</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tai_Le">Tai Le</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=67" title="Edit section: Tai Le">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/32px-Incubator-logo.svg.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="40" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/48px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/64px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="1000" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/tdd" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/tdd">Tai Nuea test</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> at <a href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wikimedia_Incubator" class="extiw" title="meta:Wikimedia Incubator">Wikimedia Incubator</a></td></tr>

<p>The <a href="/wiki/Tai_Le_alphabet" class="mw-redirect" title="Tai Le alphabet">Tai Le alphabet</a> is used for the <a href="/wiki/Tai_Nuea_language" title="Tai Nuea language">Tai Nuea language</a> (Tai Nüa). It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.gnu.org/software/freefont">GNU FreeFont</a></li>
<li>Microsoft Tai Le (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 7 and later)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansTaiLe-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Tai Le (direct download link)</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansTaiLe-Regular.ttf">(GitHub link)</a>, a font made by Google</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tai_Viet">Tai Viet</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: Tai Viet">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Tai_Dam_language#Writing_system" title="Tai Dam language">Tai Viet script</a> is used for writing the Tai languages <a href="/wiki/Tai_Dam_language" title="Tai Dam language">Tai Dam</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tai_D%C3%B3n_language" title="Tai Dón language">Tai Dón</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Thai_Song_language" title="Thai Song language">Thai Song</a>. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website-2.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansTaiViet.unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Tai Viet</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/raw/master/unhinted/NotoSansTaiViet-Regular.ttf">(GitHub link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scripts.sil.org/TaiHeritage">Tai Heritage Pro</a> from SIL International</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tangut">Tangut</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=69" title="Edit section: Tangut">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Tangut_script" title="Tangut script">Tangut script</a> was used to write the <a href="/wiki/Tangut_language" title="Tangut language">Tangut language</a>, a Tibeto-Burman language once spoken in the <a href="/wiki/Western_Xia" title="Western Xia">Western Xia</a>, also known as the Tangut Empire. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.babelstone.co.uk/Fonts/Yinchuan.html">Tangut Yinchuan</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://yedict.com/download/">TH-Tshyn-P1, TH-Feon-B</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.fontke.com/font/25861256/download/">西夏文 font download</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://github.com/googlei18n/noto-fonts/blob/master/phaseIII_only/unhinted/ttf/NotoSerifTangut/NotoSerifTangut-Regular.ttf">Noto Serif Tangut, a font made by Google </a></li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tifinagh_script">Tifinagh script</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: Tifinagh script">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Tifinagh" title="Tifinagh">Tifinagh</a> alphabet is used to write the <a href="/wiki/Berber_languages" title="Berber languages">Berber languages</a>. IRCAM (Institut Royal de la Culture Amazighe) has a software suite developed for Windows XP that contains a Tifinagh keyboard and a font available for download <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.ircam.ma/amzfr.htm">here</a>. The script is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.mondeberbere.com/langue/polices.htm">Afus Deg Wfus</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Code2000" title="Code2000">Code2000</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://dejavu-fonts.github.io/">DejaVu</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ebrima" title="Ebrima">Ebrima</a> (Microsoft Windows font, available in Windows 7 and later)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.fixedsysexcelsior.com/">Fixedsys Excelsior</a> (a stylized ornamental font, not recommended for running text)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://hapax.qc.ca/inventaire-des-oeils.htm">Hapax Berbère</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.alanwood.net/downloads/">MPH 2B Damase</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website-2.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansTifinagh-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Tifinagh (direct download link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://software.sil.org/tagmukay/">Tagmukay</a> font by  <a href="/wiki/SIL_International" title="SIL International">SIL International</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.ircam.ma/doc/polices/wintt/T_I_UNICODE.ttf">Tifinaghe-Ircam Unicode</a></li></ul>

<p>This script is used in several test wikis at the Wikimedia Incubator, including <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/tzm" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/tzm">Central Atlas Tamazight</a>, <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/shi" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/shi">Tachelhit</a> (Tasusiyt, Shilha), <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/rif" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/rif">Riffian</a>, and <a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/shy" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/shy">Shawiya</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Yi_Syllabary">Yi Syllabary</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=71" title="Edit section: Yi Syllabary">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table role="presentation" class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">
<tbody><tr>
<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/32px-Incubator-logo.svg.png" decoding="async" width="32" height="40" class="noviewer" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/48px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e3/Incubator-logo.svg/64px-Incubator-logo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="1000" /></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist"><i><b><a href="https://incubator.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wp/ii" class="extiw" title="incubator:Wp/ii">Sichuan Yi test</a></b></i> of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> at <a href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wikimedia_Incubator" class="extiw" title="meta:Wikimedia Incubator">Wikimedia Incubator</a></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p><a href="/wiki/Yi_script#Modern_Yi" title="Yi script">Modern Yi script</a> is a standardized <a href="/wiki/Syllabary" title="Syllabary">syllabary</a> derived from the classic script in 1974 by the local <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" class="mw-redirect" title="People&#39;s Republic of China">Chinese government</a>. It is used to write various <a href="/wiki/Yi_languages" class="mw-redirect" title="Yi languages">Yi languages</a>. It is supported by the following fonts:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Code2000" title="Code2000">Code2000</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_typefaces_included_with_Microsoft_Windows" title="List of typefaces included with Microsoft Windows">Microsoft Yi Baiti</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://noto-website-2.storage.googleapis.com/pkgs/NotoSansYi-unhinted.zip">Noto Sans Yi (direct download link)</a>, a font made by Google</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://scripts.sil.org/SILYI_home">Nuosu SIL</a> from SIL International</li></ul>

<th>Your browser/device
</th></tr>

</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Special_cases">Special cases</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=72" title="Edit section: Special cases">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Romanian">Romanian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=73" title="Edit section: Romanian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The Romanian alphabet contains an <a href="/wiki/S-comma" title="S-comma">S-comma</a> (Ș ș) and <a href="/wiki/T-comma" title="T-comma">T-comma</a> (Ț ț). These characters were added to Unicode 3.0 at the request of the Romanian standardization institute. As font support for these characters has been poor in the past, many computer users use the similar characters <a href="/wiki/S-cedilla" class="mw-redirect" title="S-cedilla">S-cedilla</a> (Ş ş) and <a href="/wiki/T-cedilla" class="mw-redirect" title="T-cedilla">T-cedilla</a> (Ţ ţ) instead. However, on Wikipedia it is recommended to use the correct characters with comma below.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Help:Multilingual_support&amp;action=edit&amp;section=76" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="reflist columns references-column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 30em; -webkit-column-width: 30em; column-width: 30em; list-style-type: lower-alpha;">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-1">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Until June 2005, when MediaWiki 1.5 came into use on the Wikimedia projects, articles on the English Wikipedia were encoded using <a href="/wiki/ISO/IEC_8859-1" title="ISO/IEC 8859-1">ISO/IEC 8859-1</a> (although the additional characters from the <a href="/wiki/Windows-1252" title="Windows-1252">Windows-1252</a> character set were used in practice.) All characters from the <a href="/wiki/ISO/IEC_10646" class="mw-redirect" title="ISO/IEC 10646">ISO/IEC 10646</a> Universal Character Set could be accessed through numerical entities, as specified by the HTML 4.01 specification. Since, nearly all pages have been converted to use Unicode directly. Old discussion on the topic can be read at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia_talk:Unicode" title="Wikipedia talk:Unicode">Wikipedia talk:Unicode</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-6"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-6">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Not to be confused with MS Sans Serif</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-9"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-9">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Microsoft Windows support the <i>ʾEsṭrangēlā</i> variety via Estrangelo Edessa and Segoe UI. Historically, some Linux distributions supported <i>Maḏnḥāyā</i> variety via FreeSans.</span>
</li>
</ol></div>
